 unki aakhri selleri 50 hajaar rupee he

 is prakaar inhen (formula: 33 saal + 2= 35 / 70 x15,000) ke formule ke tahat 7,500 rupee hi pension praapt hoti
 That is, under the old system, Vivek would get a monthly pension of seven and a half thousand rupees
 jabaki ab nai vyavastha main aakhri selleri ke hisaab se pension jodne par unhen 25000 hajaar rupee pension milegi
